Started abcSGP Monday February 20 00:02:32 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 00:02:32 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas

		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections

		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size

		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 01:05:41 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 01:18:53 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 01:18:53 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 02:08:49 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 02:22:10 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 03:12:04 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

		state = state.abbr
		create.additional.variables = FALSE )

	NOTE: All values of observed data reside within the LOSS/HOSS values in the SGPstateData meta-data for GA.
	NOTE: All values of observed data reside within the BOUNDARY values in the SGPstateData meta-data for GA.
	NOTE: YEAR in @Data converted from integer to character.

Finished prepareSGP Monday February 20 03:25:22 2023 in 14.972 Seconds 


Started abcSGP Monday February 20 03:25:22 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 03:25:22 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 03:38:45 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 04:15:12 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 04:15:12 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 04:28:30 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 04:28:30 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 04:41:43 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 04:41:43 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 05:18:22 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 05:31:42 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 05:31:42 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )

Started abcSGP Monday February 20 05:44:54 2023


	abcSGP(
		 sgp_object = SGP_object
		state = state.abbr
		steps = c("analyzeSGP", "combineSGP")
		sgp.percentiles = TRUE
		sgp.projections = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged = FALSE
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = FALSE
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = if (is.null(coef_matrices)) NULL else TRUE
		simulate.sgps = FALSE
		goodness.of.fit.print = FALSE
		parallel.config = list(BACKEND = "PARALLEL", WORKERS = workers)
		sgp.config = config )


Started analyzeSGP Monday February 20 05:44:54 2023


	analyzeSGP(
		 sgp_object = sgp_object
		state = state
		years = years
		content_areas = content_areas
		grades = grades
		sgp.percentiles = sgp.percentiles
		sgp.projections = sgp.projections
		sgp.projections.lagged = sgp.projections.lagged
		sgp.percentiles.baseline = sgp.percentiles.baseline
		sgp.projections.baseline = sgp.projections.baseline
		sgp.projections.lagged.baseline = sgp.projections.lagged.baseline
		sgp.minimum.default.panel.years = sgp.minimum.default.panel.years
		sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices = sgp.use.my.coefficient.matrices
		sgp.test.cohort.size = sgp.test.cohort.size
		return.sgp.test.results = return.sgp.test.results
		simulate.sgps = simulate.sgps
		calculate.simex = calculate.simex
		calculate.simex.baseline = calculate.simex.baseline
		calculate.srs = calculate.srs
		calculate.srs.baseline = calculate.srs.baseline
		goodness.of.fit.print = goodness.of.fit.print
		sgp.config = sgp.config
		parallel.config = parallel.config
		verbose.output = verbose.output
		get.cohort.data.info = get.cohort.data.info
		sgp.sqlite = sgp.sqlite
		sgp.percentiles.equated = sgp.percentiles.equated
		sgp.percentiles.equating.method = sgp.percentiles.equating.method
		sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps = sgp.percentiles.calculate.sgps
		SGPt = SGPt
		fix.duplicates = fix.duplicates )
